<text>Finally an official (Baltimore) Raven's bar downtown. Watching a Raven's game isn't quite the same unless you have other fans cheering with you. The food is really fresh and delicious. If there is something wrong, they will fix whatever the problem is. The staff want you to enjoy your visit and come back again. The vegan options are as good as every other option on the menu. Also, they have a vegan Bloody Mary mix. The bartenders are very knowledgeable about the beer options available. As they are a brewery, they have many fresh beers. They have a great points program so you earn as you drink. They created the Poe as a unique addition to their Ravens experiences. It's a milk Stout that has red currant added to it. It is discounted during Raven's games.
If football üèà isn't your thing, they have Meatless Mondays and Bingo on the 2nd Wednesday. If you're looking for a fun place, The Bell Marker is where you should be.< /text><gmap_id>0x80d954a79cf9f47b:0x42cb29f6988ee85d<//gmap_id>< name>

<review>What a great surprise to find a comfortable brewpub with vegan food options!  The pizza with sausage (made by the same people who make the Impossible burger) was the best vegan pizza I have had, you would never know it was vegan.

The Impossible burger was a nice surprise, it's always a treat to find these at any restaurant.  The beer was great, but you can find that in a lot of places in this county.  What you can't always find is friendly and efficient service.  Our waitress, Paige, was well informed and was able to guide these vegan patrons to the best foods and dessert.

Even if you can't appreciate the delicious vegan fare, this is a great spot to try.</review><name>Harper Perry<//name><Gmap_id>0x80d954a79cf9f47b:0x42cb29f6988ee85d< /Gmap_id></record>

<user>111439613671497483580<//user>< username>
David Rodriguez<//username>
<Time>1521927227582<//Time><rating>1</rating>< Review>
Just another place overselling beer in San Diego using the classic ploy of selling high percent beer and pouring it into an 8oz. glass hence more money for them and less beer for us! We do not need such practice of cunningly devicive business strategies in San Diego, especially when it comes to our beloved craft beer culture! Remember, with great power comes great responsibility. And so, either indicate on the menu (out of courtesy and consideration for your customers, if you care) which beers come in smaller glasses -or, train your staff to accordingly inform the valued customer upon ordering "The Niedermeyer" that this beer being at 9.3% ABV comes in a smaller glass. You have the power to improve and demonstrate further capacity or see how long it takes for your address to give us a real San Diego brewery who knows and cares about San Diego's craft brew culture and our beloved community. Thank you, kindly, for your consideration upon reading this. Respectfully, David R.</Review>

During the pandemic, this location of Einstein's Bagels deserves a Gold Star.  The employees deserve an A+ for operating safely and following measures to keep us customers safe.  In fact I say it is the safest eating establishment in San Diego.  They are patient with me when I call after using the app which is not perfect, to adjust my order. <gmap_id>0x80c2d5cbdcf7aa6d:0x647d81f3af996d8f<//gmap_id><user_id>111786517743281339317</user_id>< response>
None</response>
<review>Ambiance: Very, very nice. The look of the exterior of the building is already really nice, and when I first glanced at it, I thought of a high-end steakhouse or something. The interior is very modern and hip - quite like a lot of other places that seem to attract teenagers and people in their 20's. Brick walls, nice tables and chairs, candles on the shelf, nicely lit sign, outdoor patio seating, high chair seating ... I can tell that a lot of thought and money went into designing this place.

Food: I came here during their soft opening, so I'm not sure if the dishes are set in stone or subject to changing. The ramen burger looked really enticing (and pricey), but my boyfriend and I decided to just order the spam musubi. The order was $4.25 for two pieces - so pretty much around $2.00 for each. I think it was a little pricey for what I ate because while I liked the flavor of the rice and spam and the seaweed (especially what was sprinkled on the sides of the musubi), the flavor wasn't that great.

Drinks: I really wanted to order a popular drink, so I chose the potted plant milk tea with boba. My boyfriend ordered an iced green tea sea salt latte. Apparently in Chinese, the drink description said it came with a layer of milk cream at the top, which I would not have known since I don't read Chinese. We wanted to compare it to Tbay's milk cream tea - I personally thought the latte was too salty. There was a lot of sea salt that made the cream not as tasty as I would have liked, and there wasn't enough green tea flavor. For my potted plant milk tea - I actually had tried it before when my sister brought it home from Macchiato. She said it was too sweet, and I definitely agree after drinking it for myself at The Bleu House. The cream and oreo cookie crumble at the top - very sweet by itself, but it tasted better when mixed with the tea. However, it was still too sweet, and I usually don't mind sweet! The boba was cooked very well ... I really liked the texture and chewiness of the boba.

Macarons: The Bleu House's redeeming feature for me was the selection and price of the macarons. It was $1.75 each or 6 for $9.50 - great price! And the macarons are definitely quality macarons. I would say they are my third favorite coming in behind Bottega and Lette. Good flavor, great texture, wonderful flavor! I tried the rose, royal, salted caramel, vanilla, red velvet, and almond. My least favorite was the almond (haven't found one that can rival Lette's yet!), but I liked the rest a lot. Royal tasted like a royal milk tea, and the red velvet wasn't too sweet. The rose and salted caramel were my favorites - loved the texture in the middle and the shell. And they came in a little cute box! I'm glad to know they have these at Macchiato, too so I don't have to drive too far to get some when I have a craving!

Service: For the soft opening, there was a 10% discount if you checked into Yelp. They didn't advertise this, so I had to ask them if this discount was still valid. The workers are all very nice, but they seem a little confused and nervous, which is understandable. We had asked them a few questions upon ordering and upon receiving the check, and the answers they gave us didn't answer the question we had asked at all.

tl;dr - Overall, I would say this would be a nice place to sit with a friend and catch up. The small plates and entrees seem very intriguing and the prices can be justifiable depending on what you order. I probably will avoid the potted plant and just order a more common drink (or the icy)! And definitely try the macarons!<//review>< name>
Tiffany C<//name>

This house is filled with items from the 1800's. The things were not original, but were interesting none-the-less. There were rooms downstairs and upstairs. < Text>
Food is good, but they have a 3.75% "surcharge" for all credit card payments. Prices advertised is the "cash price", which is 3.75% lower. It's illegal in CA to have a surcharge for credit cards. It's OK to give a cash discount, but they need to advertise the full credit card price.

Also, I don't mind it if is like 1%, but 3.75% is a bit much, considering they already raised their food prices recently. Plenty of other BBQ joints in the area that don't do these shady business practices.<//Text>

< text>
I had the brisket plater, the brisket was extremely dry and tough. My sides were the macaroni salad which was good not great and potato salad, which was bland and disappointing as well. The garlic bread was good. The meal cost 25$ after tax and I believe was unreasonably over priced especially for the quality of the dish. I won't be back unfortunately. I had eaten here years ago the ribs and it was good however still say over priced. If looking for bbq, there is a wonderful place also close by. A brislet platter with juicy meat, delicious red potato salad coleslaw and homestyle cornbread with butter and honey for only $16 with tax is at Winchester BBQ on Winchester Blvd. About 5 to 10 minutes away. I highly recommend that restaurant I recently have gone to twice and received the same impressive quality both visits.</text>

< rating>

<text>I have been wanting to review this place for a long time but being partially a vegetarian, I thought it would be wrong to judge this place based off what I have eaten/tried so far. So I decided to put down a review based on what my husband thinks of this place. To be more accurate, we took my brother to this place to get a validation for my husband's choice!

OK Soo..If my husband had his way, this is where we would be eating every day of the week!! He loves loves loves this place (trust me, those are way less loves than his appreciation of this place).

Ambience and Staff:
The place is cosy and nice, the cutest part is that there is a toy train constantly running along the sides of the roof (Choo Choo!!)
The staff is friendly. Everytime we have visited, there was not much of a line and getting seated is pretty easy too. The restaurant has an outdoor as well an indoor seating, so you can pick what's your comfort zone.

Ordering:
Placing an order is pretty easy too, you go to the counter and get your bill. The cashier will give you your order number, you take that and pick a seat for yourself. They bring your order to the table.

Food:
For their vegetarian burger, I would give them a 2/5, the veggie patty was tasteless, there were no sauce inside the burger and it felt really dry. I got the burger with side of macaroni which was great!

Brisket: 10/10 My brother and husband both got the brisket and they would not let me rate it any less than 10/10. The meat was great, cooked well, the portion was great and the sides were amazing too. This is probably the most popular dish as most of the tables within my vision.

Needless to say, I will definitely go again and maybe this time around I can give their chicken a try!<//text>< username>
Sarah Bal</username>

<review>I had the beef ribs platter with macaroni salad and chili. I guess it was unfair of me to apply Texas BBQ standards.

The chili was mostly beans, which would have been fine if the called it BBQ beans or the like.

The ribs had good smoke, good halo, enviable glaze, and good depth of flavor in the bark. But sadly they were rushed and didn't have time to render the connective tissues so the meat would pull away from the bone.

I tasted the sauce on a spoon and it was delicious. The sides were tasty.

It is not a bad place, and may have been a rough Friday night, but I can barely give it 4 stars.

Maybe I should have tried the brisket or pork . It looked good on other people's plates.<//review>< Pictures>

<text>I ordered the Sampler Combo which is a choice of three separate items: baby back ribs, brisket, bbq pork, chicken, Italian sausage, beef ribs, hot link or Carolina style pork plus 2 sides and 1 slice of garlic bread for only $19.95. I ordered the chicken, hot link, and baby back ribs with coleslaw and baked beans as sides. Chicken and hot link were cooked perfectly but the ribs weren't as tender as I like (a little tough). The BBQ sauce was good but could have been more spicy. It was a lot of food for the price. I really liked the fact that you walk up to the counter, order, then pay immediately, and the waitresses bring the food to you. Fountain drinks are available (limited options). Overall great environment and experience. Looking forward to my next visit to try something different!</text>< pictures>

< text>
Decided to check out Sam's BBQ. today.
As I walked in from the side, I noticed that they have a inside- kinda outside seating area that looks rustic.
Walking through the doors into the main restaurant area I saw a Southern style menu board and a kitchen area behind the counter.
The inside of the restaurant is also rustic with a cool train track going around the upper inside of the restaurant.
I ordered a 1/2 slab of pork ribs that came with a slice of garlic bread and to sides. ( I chose the chili and potato salad) I also got order of there Hush puppies that come with honey butter.
Chili 2.5 stars
Potato salad (meh) 2 stars tops
Hush puppies  5 out of 5 stars so good then add the honey butter (just takes it to another level)
Pork ribs soft with plenty of meat on the bones, cooked with a BBQ sauce and glazed. 3.5 stars. Good.
Service was also good 4 stars.</text>

Secret code for BBQ experts: when you whisper "burnt ends" to the staff at this Texas joint, they know and give you what you need, quite rare and not on the published menu. Go hungry, get a beer and all the sides, do not count the calories, go home with some leftover as an evening snack. Make sure to try any of their special vegetables on the menu when possible. Lines can be long so go off hours or get takeout.

Sam's Bar-B-Que</Text>

Update: they‚Äôre certainly willing to sell you junk brisket, chewy and fatty even where it shouldn‚Äôt be... spent 28 bucks on two brisket sandwiches that were utter junk. Threw them away.

Novelty BBQ for those who haven't had real BBQ in the Carolinas, Texas, Kansas etc.  This place leans TX style-ish.
